invalid_request
The request is missing a required parameter, includes an unsupported parameter value (other than grant type), repeats a parameter, includes multiple credentials, utilizes more than one mechanism for authenticating the client, or is otherwise malformed.
AFOAuth2Manager
invalid_client
Client authentication failed (e.g., unknown client, no client authentication included, or unsupported authentication method).  The authorization server MAY return an HTTP 401 (Unauthorized) status code to indicate which HTTP authentication schemes are supported.  If the client attempted to authenticate via the "Authorization" request header field, the authorization server MUST respond with an HTTP 401 (Unauthorized) status code and include the "WWW-Authenticate" response header field matching the authentication scheme used by the client.
invalid_grant
The provided authorization grant (e.g., authorization code, resource owner credentials) or refresh token is invalid, expired, revoked, does not match the redirection URI used in the authorization request, or was issued to another client.
unauthorized_client

unsupported_grant_type

var crashlyticsOriginalOnLoad = window.onload;
var crashlyticsOriginalOnError = window.onerror;
window.onerror = crashlyticsOnError;
window.onload = crashlyticsOnLoad;
function crashlyticsOnLoad() {
    if (window.onerror != crashlyticsOnError) {
        crashlyticsOriginalOnError = window.onerror;
    }
    window.onerror = crashlyticsOnError;
    if (typeof crashlyticsOriginalOnLoad == 'function') {
        crashlyticsOriginalOnLoad();
    }
function crashlyticsOnError(msg, url, line, column, error) {
    var string = "crashlytics://exception/uiwebkit?msg=";
    string += encodeURIComponent(msg);
    string += "&url=";
    string += encodeURIComponent(url);
    string += "&line=";
    string += encodeURIComponent(line);
    if (column) {
        string += "&column=";
        string += encodeURIComponent(column);
    }
    crashlyticsExecute(string);
    if (typeof crashlyticsOriginalOnError == 'function') {
        crashlyticsOriginalOnError(msg, url, line, column, error);
    }
function crashlyticsExecute(url) {
    var iframe = document.createElement("IFRAME");
    iframe.setAttribute("src", url);
    document.documentElement.appendChild(iframe);
    iframe.parentNode.removeChild(iframe);
    iframe = null;
"loaded"
function crashlyticsOnError(msg, url, line, column, error) {
    var message = {
        msg: msg,
        url: url,
        line: line,
        column: column
    }
    window.webkit.messageHandlers.crashlytics.postMessage(message);
    if (typeof crashlyticsOriginalOnError == 'function') {
        crashlyticsOriginalOnError(msg, url, line, column, error);
    }
